< text>
The service was mediocre to say the least....if you have multiple customers in line, don't just stand there and ignore them for a few minutes. Usually when you get called for your order to go they at least ask if you want any ketchup or sauce...nope.
The food was terrible. Ordered a number 1 (famous star meal)...they put so much mayo and ketchup on the burger that the bun was mushy and falling apart before I even fully unwrapped the burger. They didn't even spread out the toppings. One spot had only onions, one spot had only tomatoes and one spot had only pickles. When they did call my order and I asked for ketchup, he gave me a handful...the only problem was the outside of the packets were covered in a syrup-like sticky substance.
Home of the $6 burger....more like home of the mush patty.
I know it's fast food, so I shouldn't expect much. But I was a paying customer. Regardless of what your job is, good customer service should be important.
Won't be eating at Carl's Jr. anymore.<//text>

<Text>Perfect for trail run but parking is horrible. I park a mile away and run from there to avoid the frustration of not getting a parking spot. I actually like that better, because I can add a total of 2 miles on my run. It is a really lovely place to run; we usually run on Woods Trail, Umumhum, Santa Teresa, and Quicksiver. This is one of my of my favorite runs when I can do it :) There are plenty of trails so it's easy to decide if you want a long one or a short one, tough or easy. There are also nice restroom facilities which is a plus as not all Open Space Reserves have restroom facilities. If you haven't checked it out, do it, you won't be disappointed. I gave it a 4 star because of the parking issue...< /Text>< Pictures>

I believe more fish are caught during the day as opposed to the evening, but there seems to be a consistent  group of people who fish late at night.< /Review>
